Overview Notes: Raised insulin: when the pancreas makes more insulin to process high levels of carbohydrates in the blood.Diabetes develops when pancreas cant make large amounts of insulin needed for normal blood sugar, reduce carb intake

Jashwin thank you for coming for the medical, well done with all your efforts made so far, I know you will keep improving, hope these tips help you optimise your health.
